### [101] [Masked Language Flow Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27617)
*Iskander Azangulov,Kianoosh Ashouritaklimi,Leo Zhang,Simon Vary,Patrick Rebeschini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Masked Language Flow Models (MLFMs)，通过引入连续随机插值将掩码机制融入流语言模型（FLMs），实现条件生成与单步推理。结合连续去噪与置信度高的离散解掩码，支持多步推理，并可将预训练的掩码扩散模型轻量级转换为MLFMs。在GSM8K和MT-Bench上验证了其在推理与指令遵循任务中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有流语言模型（FLMs）在多步推理中需逐个生成所有标记的问题，同时克服掩码扩散模型（MDMs）在少步采样时因独立位置假设导致性能下降的局限性。

Method: 引入连续随机插值以连接部分掩码序列与完整序列，构建可条件生成的连续流；设计交替进行连续去噪与离散解掩码的新采样策略；通过轻量级适配将预训练的MDMs转化为MLFMs。

Result: 首次证明基于流的语言模型可在复杂推理和指令遵循任务中有效扩展，显著提升多步推理能力，在GSM8K和MT-Bench上表现优于传统方法。

Conclusion: MLFMs结合了流模型的高效生成与掩码模型的灵活性，实现了快速、可扩展的条件语言生成，为流式语言建模在复杂任务中的应用开辟新路径。

Abstract: Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs) promise fast, parallel language generation, but their reverse transition factorises across token positions -- an approximation that breaks down in the few-step sampling regime where parallel generation ought to provide the greatest efficiency gains. Flow Language Models (FLMs) sidestep this limitation by learning a continuous flow that transports noise toward clean sequences represented in Euclidean space, inducing a flow map that can be distilled for single-step generation. However, this makes complex tasks requiring multi-step reasoning problematic for FLMs, as FLMs are forced to decode every token during generation. To address this, we introduce Masked Language Flow Models (MLFMs), which incorporate masking into FLMs using a continuous stochastic interpolant to bridge partially masked and clean sequences. This design enables conditional generation via continuous flows and allows pretrained MDMs to be converted into MLFMs through a simple, lightweight adaptation. Leveraging this flexibility, we propose a novel sampler that alternates continuous denoising with the discrete unmasking of confident tokens to better support multi-step reasoning. We evaluate our approach on GSM8K and MT-Bench and find, for the first time, that flow-based language models can be scaled to solve downstream reasoning and instruction-following tasks.

Second, a three-class fine-labeled test set covering Weibo, Xiaohongshu, Tieba, and Zhihu is constructed, domain distances from the source are quantified using Jaccard and Proxy-A Distance, as well as the degradation bottleneck of the baseline under domain shift is systematically revealed. Herein, a dual threshold hard example mining strategy is proposed. High- and low-confidence error-prone samples are filtered from unlabeled corpora by prediction confidence. The model is secondarily finetuned under implicit contexts with merely a small set of manually labeled hard examples, realizing low-cost cross-platform domain adaptation. Experiments reveal significant performance gains of the optimized model across four platforms.

### [103] [Yuvion LLM: An Adversarially-Aware Large Language Model for Content And AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27632)

TL;DR: Yuvion LLM 是一种专为对抗鲁棒性内容安全和更广泛的人工智能安全设计的大语言模型，通过对抗感知数据构建、知识增强的持续预训练以及基于策略的安全多任务后训练等方法，显著提升了在复杂安全场景下的鲁棒性和安全性。其配套的 YLRE 评估基准涵盖93个任务，全面测试安全、对抗鲁棒性和现实能力。实验表明，Yuvion-8B 在多项安全任务上超越多个更大规模的基线模型，包括 GPT-5.4 和 Qwen3-MAX。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Yuvion LLM 的构建流程包括：对抗感知的数据构造、知识增强的持续预训练、基于策略的多任务安全后训练（含风险感知监督微调与强化学习策略优化），以及面向工具使用和多步推理的安全感知代理强化学习。同时引入 YLRE 评估集，覆盖四类共93项基准测试，聚焦于安全、对抗鲁棒性和实际应用能力。

Result: 在多种安全基准测试中，Yuvion LLM 表现优异，尤其在对抗条件下展现出强鲁棒性；同时保持良好的整体能力。其中，Yuvion-8B 模型在多个安全任务上优于 GPT-5.4、Qwen3-MAX 等更大规模的先进模型。

Conclusion: Yuvion LLM 成功将对抗鲁棒性与代理能力作为核心设计目标，在保障安全的同时实现了高阶功能表现，为真实世界中更可靠的大语言模型部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: As large language models are increasingly deployed in real-world systems, safety failures can still lead to harmful outputs and dangerous misuse. We argue that the essence of safety is adversarial: many failures arise not from natural inputs alone, but from strategic attempts to evade model policies and safeguards. However, existing general-purpose model development largely overlook this adversarial nature, and often remain insufficient for realistic safety scenarios involving planning, tool use, and multi-step reasoning, causing measured safety performance to overestimate real deployment robustness. To address this gap, we present Yuvion LLM, a large language model built for adversarially robust content safety and broader AI safety. Yuvion LLM treats adversarial robustness and agentic capability as first-class objectives. Its pipeline combines adversarially aware data construction, knowledge-enhanced continued pretraining, and policy-grounded multi-task safety post-training, including risk-aware supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning-based policy optimization, together with safety-aware agentic reinforcement learning for tool use and multi-step reasoning in complex safety scenarios. We further introduce the Yuvion LLM RiskEval (YLRE), a collection of 93 benchmarks across four evaluation categories, covering diverse open and internal evaluations with a focus on safety, adversarial robustness, and real-world capability requirements. Across these evaluations, Yuvion LLM demonstrates clear advantages on safety-focused benchmarks and particularly strong robustness under adversarial conditions, while maintaining solid overall capability. Notably, Yuvion-8B outperforms most state-of-the-art baselines, including substantially larger models such as GPT-5.4 and Qwen3-MAX, on several safety tasks.

### [104] [When Search Agents Should Ask: DiscoBench for Clarification-Aware Deep Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27669)
*Yiling Tao,Shihan Deng,Meiling Tao,Pengzhi Wei,Zhichao Hu,Zhihao Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 DiscoBench，一个用于评估搜索代理在存在模糊性时能否主动识别问题、提出有效澄清问题并借助用户交互恢复正确推理路径的基准。该基准包含211个样本和463个模糊实例，覆盖11个真实世界领域，涵盖四种模糊类型。通过设计多轮交互用户模拟器，从任务实用性、模糊识别、交互策略和成本效率四个维度评估模型表现。实验表明，模糊识别与有效澄清是两种独立能力，重复搜索而非提问往往比直接猜测更差，揭示了当前搜索代理在检索能力与交互式问题解决之间存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建 DiscoBench 基准，包含211个样本和463个模糊实例，覆盖11个真实世界领域，涵盖四种模糊类型；设计多轮交互用户模拟器；从任务实用性、模糊检测、交互策略、成本效率四个角度评估主流LLM的表现。

Result: 实验显示，模糊检测与有效澄清是两个独立的能力；重复搜索而不提问的策略往往比直接猜测效果更差；当前搜索代理在检索能力与交互式问题解决能力之间存在明显差距。

Conclusion: DiscoBench 为评估搜索代理在复杂、模糊环境下的交互式推理能力提供了重要基准。研究揭示了现有模型在主动澄清与高效交互方面存在明显短板，强调需将交互智能纳入下一代搜索系统设计的核心。

Abstract: Search agents powered by large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to solve complex information-seeking tasks, requiring multi-step retrieval and reasoning to fulfill user goals. However, existing benchmarks often assume that user queries are complete and explicit, overlooking the fact that real-world search requests are frequently vague, underspecified, or even factually incorrect. In deep search scenarios, such ambiguity can propagate along multi-step reasoning chains and lead agents toward incorrect search trajectories. To address this gap, we introduce DiscoBench, a benchmark for clarification-aware deep search, designed to evaluate whether search agents can proactively identify ambiguity, ask effective clarification questions, and recover correct reasoning paths through user interaction. DiscoBench contains 211 samples and 463 ambiguity instances across 11 real-world domains, covering four ambiguity types. We further design a user simulator for multi-turn interaction and evaluate model performance from four perspectives: task utility, ambiguity detection, interaction strategy, and cost efficiency. Experiments on representative LLMs show that ambiguity detection and effective clarification are distinct capabilities, and that repeatedly searching instead of asking for clarification often performs worse than direct guessing, highlighting a critical gap between retrieval ability and interactive problem-solving in current search agents.

### [105] [From Signals to Transfer: A Factorised Study of Probe-Based Uncertainty Estimation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27679)
*Ponhvoan Srey,Xiaobao Wu,Cong-Duy Nguyen,Quang Minh Nguyen,Duc Anh Vu,Anh Tuan Luu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在一致条件下对基于探针的不确定性估计（UE）进行分解研究的方法，以解决现有方法在特征设计、训练数据构建和评估设置上的多样性导致性能驱动因素不明确的问题。研究发现，原始隐藏状态和注意力特征在域内表现尚可，但在分布外情况下，结构化和压缩特征更具鲁棒性，表明仅依赖域内性能不足以衡量进展。此外，提示方式和标签构建显著影响探针行为。基于这些发现，作者训练了可迁移性较好的基准预训练探针，适用于开放式事实生成任务，提供了一个稳定的开箱即用基线，推动更面向部署的探针式不确定性估计评估。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于探针的不确定性估计方法在特征设计、训练数据构建和评估设置上存在较大差异，难以判断真正影响性能的因素，亟需在统一条件下进行系统性分析，以指导实际应用和模型改进。

Method: 提出一种因子分解研究框架，在相同实验条件下对比不同特征类型（如原始隐藏状态、注意力特征、结构化与压缩特征）、提示策略及标签构造方式对探针性能的影响，通过控制变量法识别关键影响因素。

Result: 原始隐藏状态和注意力特征在域内表现良好，但在分布外场景下表现较差；而结构化和压缩特征在分布外更具鲁棒性；提示方式和标签构造对探针行为有显著影响；基于最佳实践训练的基准探针在开放生成任务中表现出良好的迁移能力。

Conclusion: 仅依赖域内性能无法全面评估不确定性估计器的有效性，应重视分布外鲁棒性和实际部署场景下的表现；建议采用标准化的基准探针作为稳定基线，并推动更贴近实际应用的评估范式。

Abstract: Probe-based uncertainty estimation (UE) has emerged as a prominent approach to detect hallucinations in Large Language Models (LLMs) by learning uncertainty from internal model signals. Yet, recent methods vary simultaneously across feature design, training data construction, and evaluation setting, obscuring what actually drives performance. To address this issue, we propose a factorised study of probe-based UE under matched conditions. Our results show that raw hidden states and attention features are difficult to outperform in-domain. However, under distribution shift, structured and compressed features are more robust, suggesting that in-domain performance alone is insufficient to measure progress. Furthermore, prompting and label construction significantly affect probe behaviour. Building on these best-practice findings, we train benchmark-based pretrained probes that transfer reasonably well to open-ended factual generation, providing a stable off-the-shelf baseline. Our work encourages more deployment-oriented evaluation of probe-based uncertainty estimators. The code repository is available at https://github.com/ponhvoan/ProbeUE.

</details>


### [106] [Mitigating LLM-based p-Hacking by Preregistering for the Next LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27687)
*Maria Thomas,Kristina Gligoric,Nihar B. Shah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种协议以缓解大语言模型（LLM）研究中的p-hacking问题，通过预注册实验和可接受的模型列表，并在预注册后首个符合条件的模型发布时运行确认性分析。该方法确保所用模型在承诺时并不存在，从而无法针对其进行操控；同时，针对一个模型的配置优化通常不适用于下一个模型。在两个已知真实值的任务上评估表明，该协议在73.9%和72.7%的情况下阻止了p-hack的转移。进一步的压力测试显示其有效性依然显著。作者还亲自遵循该协议进行预注册，结果证实：在6种曾成功攻击前一模型的配置中，未能在后续首个合格模型上实现成功攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数据生成、分类和标注中广泛应用，但其研究易受p-hacking影响，研究人员可通过调整提示词、解码参数或输出格式来人为获得期望结果。现有方法缺乏对模型选择与参数调优的约束机制，导致结果不可靠。因此需要一种可抵御人为操纵的系统性协议。

Method: 提出一种基于预注册的协议：研究者先在当前模型上确定分析流程，预注册分析计划及一组未来可能使用的合格模型；随后在预注册后首个符合条件的模型发布时执行确认性分析。由于目标模型在预注册时尚未存在，无法针对性地设计欺骗策略；且不同模型间的有效配置通常不具有可迁移性。

Result: 在20个来自四个提供商的模型和11种不同分析配置下，该协议在两个任务中分别阻止了73.9%和72.7%的p-hack转移。压力测试显示其鲁棒性强。作者实际应用该协议进行预注册，结果显示原本在前一模型上成功的6种配置均未能在新模型上复制成功。

Conclusion: 所提出的预注册协议能有效降低大语言模型研究中的p-hacking风险，提升研究结果的可信度。该方法利用模型迭代的不可预测性与配置的非可迁移性，为自动化研究提供了一种可靠的验证机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate, classify, and annotate data whose outputs feed downstream hypothesis tests. However, LLM-based research is easy to p-hack: a researcher can tune the prompts, decoding parameters, or output format until a desired result is reached. We propose a protocol to mitigate p-hacking in LLM-based research: preregistering the experiment and eligible models, and then running it on the first eligible LLM that is released after the preregistration. The researcher finalizes the procedure on current models, preregisters the analysis plan together with a set of eligible future models, and runs the confirmatory analysis on the first eligible model released afterward. Because this model does not exist at commitment time, it cannot be hacked against; furthermore, configurations that hack one model frequently do not transfer to the next. We evaluate the protocol on two tasks whose true values are known. Across 20 models from four providers and 11 LLM-analysis configurations, the protocol would have blocked successful transfer of the p-hack in 73.9% and 72.7% of cases in the two tasks. Additional analyses reveal that mitigation remains substantial under several stress tests. Finally, putting money where our mouth is, we followed our own protocol and preregistered our experiment. The preregistered experiment confirmed the protocol's effectiveness: out of the 7 configurations that hacked the prior model, the hacking failed to carry over in 6 configurations on the first eligible model released afterward.

</details>


### [107] [Mitigating Position Bias in Transformers via Layer-Specific Positional Embedding Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27705)
*Changze Lv,Zhenghua Wang,Yiran Ding,Yixin Wu,Tianlong Li,Zhibo Xu,Muling Wu,Tianyuan Shi,Shizheng Li,Qi Qian,Xuanjing Huang,Xiaoqing Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种分层位置嵌入缩放（LPES）方法，通过为每一层分配不同的缩放因子来解决大语言模型在长上下文中的“中间丢失”问题。采用基于贝塞尔曲线的遗传算法高效搜索最优缩放因子，显著降低搜索空间，无需微调参数且不增加推理延迟。实验表明，LPES有效缓解了位置注意力偏差，在多个长上下文基准上均取得一致提升，关键值检索任务最高提升11.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过多尺度旋转位置编码（RoPE）缓解长上下文中的信息丢失问题，但存在高延迟或依赖次优手工缩放策略的局限性。

Method: 提出层特定位置嵌入缩放（LPES），为每层分配独立缩放因子，并使用结合贝塞尔曲线的遗传算法优化各层缩放因子选择，以减少搜索空间并保持高效推理。

Result: LPES有效缓解了位置注意力偏差，在多个长上下文基准测试中表现优异，关键值检索任务最高实现11.2%的准确率提升，且无需额外训练或增加推理延迟。

Conclusion: LPES是一种高效、无须微调且低延迟的解决方案，可显著改善大语言模型在长上下文任务中的表现，尤其适用于对中间信息敏感的应用场景。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) still struggle with the ``lost-in-the-middle'' problem, where critical information located in the middle of long-context inputs is often underrepresented or lost. While existing methods attempt to address this by combining multi-scale rotary position embeddings (RoPE), they typically suffer from high latency or rely on suboptimal hand-crafted scaling strategies. To overcome these limitations, we introduce a layer-specific positional embedding scaling~(LPES) method that assigns distinct scaling factors to each layer. LPES achieves a more balanced attention distribution without fine-tuning model parameters or increasing inference delay. A specially designed genetic algorithm is employed to efficiently select the optimal scaling factors for each layer by incorporating Bézier curves to significantly reduce the search space. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LPES effectively mitigates positional attention bias and delivers consistent improvements across multiple long-context benchmarks, yielding up to an $11.2$\% accuracy gain on the key-value retrieval dataset.

Method: 引入一种基于角色的重写管道，将用户话语与低随和性情境关联，并配以温暖、缓和的助手回应；通过三组实验在四个模型上验证其效果，并使用表示探针分析潜在的表征变化。

Conclusion: 通过数据设计即可实现更安全的共情微调，无需额外的安全标注、检测机制或改变训练目标，证明了安全共情微调的可行性。

Abstract: Recent work has shown that fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) for social warmth degrades factual reliability and increases sycophancy. We investigate a related but distinct failure mode: warmth fine-tuning also weakens adversarial safety, making models more susceptible to jailbreaks and harmful output generation. We examine whether this reflects an inherent consequence of empathetic adaptation or an artifact of data construction. To address this, we introduce a persona-driven rewriting pipeline that conditions user turns on low agreeableness and pairs this with warm, de-escalating assistant responses. Across three experiments on four models, our approach reduces jailbreak susceptibility and harmful output rates relative to generic warmth fine-tuning baselines, while preserving conversational warmth. Representational probing provides suggestive evidence that this conditioning reduces the geometric alignment between warmth and compliance directions in latent space. These results show that safer empathetic fine-tuning is achievable through data design alone, without safety labels, harm detectors, or changes to the training objective.

### [109] [Do Speech Emphasis Models Generalize across Languages and Emotions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27717)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 单语模型在跨语言情境下表现差，尤其在语言类型差异较大的情况下性能显著下降；多语言训练显著提升了模型的鲁棒性。模型在高唤醒与低唤醒情绪之间具备良好的迁移能力。合成基准与感知基准之间的双向迁移表明两者共享相似的韵律结构。即使在小规模训练数据下，模型性能仍保持稳定，表现出较强的可扩展性。

Conclusion: MMEE数据集为多语言多情感强调检测提供了高质量基准。多语言训练是提升模型泛化能力的关键。韵律特征在不同情感和语言间具有共性，支持跨域迁移。该研究推动了强调检测从单一语境向真实复杂表达场景的演进。

Abstract: Prosodic emphasis varies across languages, emotions, and speaking styles, yet existing emphasis detection models are largely trained and evaluated on monolingual neutral read speech. We introduce MMEE (Multilingual Multi-Emotion Emphasis), a corpus of 10,000 professionally recorded expressive utterances (14.13 hours) across 7 languages and 34 emotion/style categories, with three-level perceptual labels (10 annotations per sample). We benchmark two state-of-the-art architectures under monolingual, cross-lingual, multilingual, cross-emotion, cross-dataset, and data-scale settings. Monolingual models show limited zero-shot transfer, degrading across typologically distant languages, while multilingual training substantially improves robustness. Models transfer robustly between high- and low-arousal emotions; bidirectional transfer between synthetic and perceptual benchmarks suggests shared prosodic structure; and performance stays robust even at smaller training scales.

### [110] [Enhancing Numerical Prediction in LLMs via Smooth MMD Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27731)
*Zhuo Zuo,Li Yue,Wenhao Zheng,Chenpeng Wang,Xianggen Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Smooth Maximum Mean Discrepancy (SMMD)损失函数，用于提升大语言模型在数值任务中的精确性。传统交叉熵忽略数值的度量结构，而SMMD通过引入基于数值距离的核函数和图平滑机制，使预测分布与目标分布对齐，并增强局部一致性。在数学推理、算术计算、时钟识别和图表问答等任务上，SMMD显著优于交叉熵及现有数值目标损失函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在需要数值精确的任务中表现不可靠，主要因为标准交叉熵将数值标记视为无结构类别，忽略了数值之间的度量关系。因此，亟需一种能捕捉数值语义距离的训练目标。

Method: 提出SMMD损失，基于经典MMD，设计值距离核函数并构建数值子词汇上的核图，通过核匹配对齐预测与目标分布，并利用图平滑机制约束预测-目标残差，实现局部一致性。

Result: 在四个数值任务上，SMMD在多个开源大模型和视觉语言模型上均取得一致性能提升，且分析表明核设计与平滑机制具有互补作用。

Conclusion: SMMD有效缓解了大模型在数值任务中的不准确性问题，证明了基于度量结构的损失函数设计的重要性，为高精度数值生成提供了新思路。

Abstract: Despite their strong general capabilities, large language models (LLMs) often remain unreliable when outputs must be numerically precise. A key reason is the training objective: standard cross-entropy treats numeric tokens as unstructured categories and ignores the metric structure of their values. We address this mismatch with Smooth Maximum Mean Discrepancy (SMMD), which builds on the classic MMD by incorporating value-distance kernels over numeric tokens and graph-based smoothness. With this kernel defined over a numeric sub-vocabulary, SMMD aligns the predicted numeric distribution to the target via kernel matching and smooths the prediction-target residual over the induced kernel graph to encourage local consistency. We evaluate SMMD on four numeric-target tasks: mathematical reasoning, arithmetic calculation, clock-time recognition, and chart question answering, across multiple open-weight LLM and VLM backbones. SMMD consistently improves accuracy over both cross-entropy and recent numeric-target losses; analyses show complementary effects between MMD and smoothness and underscore the importance of distance-based kernel design. Code is available at https://github.com/Zuozhuo/smmd-loss.

</details>


### [111] [KG2Cypher: Data-Centric Pipeline for Building Enterprise Text-to-Cypher Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27742)
*Minjun Choi,Yerin Kim,Junghyuk Seo,Sujin Mo,Hyemin Lee,Youngjoong Ko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: KG2Cypher 是一种数据驱动的流水线，用于从现有企业知识图谱（KG）构建自然语言到 Cypher 查询的系统。它通过生成可执行的 Cypher 查询并利用大语言模型（LLM）生成对应自然语言问题，形成文本-Cypher 对，并经过 LLM 判断和人工验证后转化为候选感知的监督微调（SFT）数据。系统采用类别条件化模式提示、实体检索和基于 LoRA 的推理进行部署。在韩语企业场景中，该方法显著提升了查询执行结果的 F1 分数，在 11 类任务中达到 95.2% 精确匹配率、99.9% 执行率和 0.964 的执行结果 F1，有效应对短查询和模式重述带来的语言对齐挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建企业级自然语言接口成本高昂，尤其在短查询和模式重述频繁的场景下，语言与图结构之间的对齐困难。因此需要一种高效、低成本的方法来生成高质量的文本到 Cypher 查询数据，以支持企业内部搜索与问答系统。

Method: KG2Cypher 首先基于图谱事实构造可执行的 Cypher 查询，再使用 LLM 生成对应的自然语言问题；生成的文本-Cypher 对经由 LLM 判定与人工校验，转化为候选感知的 SFT 数据；训练后的生成器结合类别条件化模式提示、实体检索和 LoRA 微调进行推理，提升准确性和效率。

Result: 在韩语企业环境中，LoRA 微调使广播节目类查询的执行结果 F1 从 0.806 提升至 0.950，公司类查询从 0.70 提升至 0.92；在 11 类分类设置下，系统实现 95.2% 精确匹配率、99.9% 执行率和 0.964 的执行结果 F1，表现优异。

Conclusion: KG2Cypher 为构建企业级文本到 Cypher 接口提供了一种高效、可扩展的数据驱动方案，能够有效应对语言歧义与模式复杂性挑战，显著提升查询系统的准确性与实用性。

Abstract: Enterprise Knowledge Graphs (KGs) are increasingly used for internal search, analytics, and question answering, but building natural-language interfaces for private enterprise graphs remains costly. We present KG2Cypher, a data-centric pipeline for building enterprise text-to-Cypher systems from existing KGs. KG2Cypher first constructs an executable Cypher query from observed graph facts and then uses LLMs to generate its associated natural-language question. The resulting Text-Cypher pairs are validated with an LLM judge and human validation, and are converted into candidate-aware SFT data. The trained generator is served with class-conditioned schema prompting, entity retrieval, and LoRA-based inference. We evaluate KG2Cypher in Korean enterprise settings, where short search-style queries and schema paraphrases make language grounding difficult. LoRA SFT improves execution-result F1 from 0.806 to 0.950 on broadcast-program queries and from 0.70 to 0.92 on company queries. In an 11-class setting, KG2Cypher achieves 95.2% exact match, 99.9% execution rate, and 0.964 execution-result F1.

</details>


### [112] [Output-Space Allocation Costs for Calibration-Guided LLM Compression: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27785)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ROCKET-ActCost, which aligns the MCKP allocation cost with output-space objectives, improves zero-shot accuracy by +0.8% on Qwen3-8B at 50% compression but worsens perplexity, revealing a tradeoff between metrics. The high correlation between weight-space and output-space errors limits divergence, explaining the modest gains. At lower compression (20%) on Llama-3.2-1B, both methods perform nearly identically.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate whether aligning the allocation cost in training-free LLM compression with output-space objectives improves model fidelity, as current methods use weight-space Frobenius error which may not fully reflect downstream performance.

Method: ROCKET-ActCost modifies the ROCKET framework by replacing the weight-space Frobenius error with an output-space reconstruction objective in the multi-choice knapsack problem (MCKP) allocation step, while retaining sparse-dictionary factorization for per-layer compression.

Result: On Qwen3-8B at 50% compression, ROCKET-ActCost achieves 53.1% average zero-shot accuracy (vs 52.3% for ROCKET) but has higher WikiText perplexity (61.46 vs 52.98). On Llama-3.2-1B at 20% compression, results are nearly identical (53.3% vs 53.5% accuracy, 14.45 vs 14.66 PPL).

Conclusion: Aligning allocation cost with output-space objectives can improve certain downstream metrics like accuracy, but introduces tradeoffs such as increased perplexity. The strong correlation between weight-space and output-space errors limits the benefit, especially at lower compression ratios.

Abstract: Training-free compression methods for large language models (LLMs) often use calibration data to guide compression decisions. ROCKET, a recent method combining sparse-dictionary factorization with multi-choice knapsack problem (MCKP) allocation, derives its per-layer factorization from an output reconstruction objective but uses weight-space Frobenius error as the MCKP allocation cost. We investigate whether aligning the allocation cost with the output-space objective improves compressed model fidelity. On Qwen3-8B at 50\% compression, our ROCKET-ActCost achieves +0.8 percentage points higher average accuracy across 8 zero-shot benchmarks (53.1\% vs 52.3\%), but increases WikiText perplexity by 16\% (61.46 vs 52.98). This accuracy-perplexity tradeoff reveals that different allocation objectives favor different downstream metrics. The high correlation ($>$0.99) between weight-space and output-space errors limits allocation divergence, explaining the modest effect size. On Llama-3.2-1B at 20\% compression, the two methods produce near-identical results (53.3\% vs 53.5\% accuracy, 14.45 vs 14.66 PPL), suggesting that the effect of the cost function is minor at lower compression ratios.

</details>


### [113] [SHIFT: Gate-Modulated Activation Steering for Knowledge Conflict Mitigation in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27786)
*Ruochang Li,Pengcheng Huang,Zhenghao Liu,Yukun Yan,Huiyuan Xie,Yu Gu,Ge Yu,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SHIFT框架，通过可学习门控调制将神经元级修改转化为自适应调节机制，以解决检索增强生成（RAG）系统中外部上下文与参数化知识之间的冲突问题。该方法仅需优化不到0.01%的可训练参数，保持主干模型冻结，通过轻量级门控模块动态调整内部表示，实现对上下文与参数知识的灵活利用。在六个数据集上的实验验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于神经元级修改的方法虽能缓解知识冲突，但可能因神经元功能纠缠引发连锁副作用，损害模型整体能力。因此需要一种更安全、可控且高效的知识冲突解决机制。

Method: 提出SHIFT框架，将神经元级修改转化为可学习门控调制，引入轻量级门控模块，仅微调极少量参数（<0.01%），在推理时动态调节内部激活，实现对上下文与参数知识的自适应融合。

Result: 在六个不同数据集上，SHIFT显著优于多种基线方法，在缓解知识冲突的同时保持了模型的通用性能，且参数开销极低。

Conclusion: SHIFT通过可学习门控机制实现了对知识冲突的有效调控，是一种高效、低侵入性的解决方案，为RAG系统中的知识融合提供了新思路。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) enhances LLMs by incorporating external knowledge to support response generation. However, conflicts between retrieved context and parametric knowledge have emerged as a critical challenge in RAG systems. To mitigate such conflicts, numerous studies have attempted to identify and edit knowledge-related internal neurons, aiming to improve the ability of LLMs to rely on contextual evidence during generation. However, these neuron-level approaches may introduce unintended cascading effects that compromise the general capabilities of LLMs, as the modified neurons are often entangled with broader model behaviors and functionalities. In this paper, we introduce SHIFT, a novel framework that reformulates neuron-level modification as learnable gate modulation, allowing LLMs to adaptively regulate internal activations for knowledge conflict resolution. Technically, our SHIFT equips LLMs with a lightweight gate module and optimizes fewer than 0.01% trainable parameters while keeping the backbone model frozen. During generation, the gate module adjusts the model's internal representations to adaptively leverage contextual and parametric knowledge. Extensive experiments on six datasets validate the effectiveness of our SHIFT in comparison with various competing baselines. All datasets and code are available at https://github.com/OpenBMB/SHIFT.

### [114] [NLL-Guided Full-Attention Layer Selection for Training-Free Sliding-Window Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27791)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种无需训练的NLL引导层选择方法，通过计算每层在使用滑动窗口注意力时对答案词元的负对数似然下降程度，来衡量其重要性。该方法在LongMemEval上仅用1/4全注意力层即达到64.6%准确率，匹配1/2全注意力周期基线，同时将计算成本减半，显著优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合注意力模型中，如何确定哪些层应保留全注意力仍是一个未解问题，传统固定周期或基于注意力的启发式方法可能无法有效捕捉下游任务准确性所需的关键信息。

Method: 提出NLL-guided layer selection方法，通过评估每层在切换为滑动窗口注意力时对负对数似然的影响，量化其重要性，并据此选择关键层保留全注意力。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B模型和LongMemEval数据集上，仅使用1/4全注意力层即可实现64.6%准确率，优于周期性1/4-FA基线10.4个百分点，且计算量减半；消融分析表明该信号与长程依赖需求一致。

Conclusion: NLL引导层选择是一种高效、低成本的训练自由方法，仅需约15分钟校准，显著提升了长上下文大模型部署中的效率-精度权衡性能。

Abstract: Hybrid attention models that mix full and sliding-window attention across layers offer a promising approach to efficient long-context inference, but the critical question of \emph{which layers} should retain full attention remains unsolved. Existing methods use either fixed periodic patterns or attention-based heuristics that may not capture what matters for downstream accuracy. We propose NLL-guided layer selection, a training-free method that directly measures each layer's importance by computing the negative log-likelihood degradation on answer tokens when that layer uses sliding-window instead of full attention. On LongMemEval with Qwen3-4B, our method achieves 64.6\% accuracy using only 1/4 full-attention layers, matching the 1/2-FA periodic baseline (65.0\%) while halving the computational budget. NLL-guided selection outperforms the SWAA-reported periodic 1/4-FA baseline by 10.4 percentage points and a matched LightTransfer-style baseline by 26.4 percentage points. De-confounding analysis shows the signal is consistent with long-range attention needs rather than generic layer sensitivity. The method requires only $\sim$15 minutes of one-time calibration, advancing the efficiency-accuracy Pareto frontier for long-context LLM deployment.

### [115] [Position Bias Correction is Insufficient for One-Pass Attention Sorting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27793)
*Qiong Tang,Xiangkun Hu,Xiangyang Liu,Yiran Chen,Yunfan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Debiased One-Pass Attention Sorting以解决长上下文语言模型中的位置偏差问题，通过单次排序修正注意力分数，但实验表明该方法在多数情况下无法达到迭代排序的效果，说明位置偏差并非唯一瓶颈，重复重排本身具有额外优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文语言模型存在位置偏差，中间位置信息利用不足；现有Attention Sorting虽有效但需多次排序-生成循环，增加部署成本。

Method: 提出基于注意力模式估计位置偏差曲线，并通过减法或除法校正原始注意力分数，实现单次排序。

Result: 在LLaMA-2-7B-32K-Instruct上，去偏效果与未校准的单次排序无差异（94.83%包含准确率）；在YaRN-Llama-2-7b-64k上，去偏提升8.67个百分点，但仍落后于迭代排序14.84个百分点，仅弥补37%差距。

Abstract: Long-context language models suffer from position bias, where information in middle positions is underutilized. Attention Sorting addresses this by iteratively reordering documents based on attention patterns, but its multiple sort-and-generate cycles increase deployment cost. We hypothesize that position bias is the primary bottleneck and propose Debiased One-Pass Attention Sorting, which estimates a per-prompt position-bias curve from the low-attention majority of documents and uses it to correct raw attention scores (via subtraction or division) to enable single-pass sorting. Our experiments on two models refute this hypothesis in the tested setting: on LLaMA-2-7B-32K-Instruct, debiasing produces identical results to uncalibrated single-pass sorting (94.83\% containment accuracy), while on YaRN-Llama-2-7b-64k, debiasing improves accuracy by 8.67 percentage points but remains 14.84pp behind iterative sorting, closing only 37\% of the gap. These results suggest that position-bias correction is insufficient to match iterative sorting, and that repeated reordering provides additional benefits beyond bias correction.

Method: 采用候选匹配与受控Seq2Seq生成方法，在德语汽车维护数据集上分析互补动作建模。重点控制动作短语层面的修改，并结合检索、重叠度与人工评估进行关系正确性评价。

Abstract: A minute lexical variation can reverse the procedural meaning of an instruction even when the rest of the sentence remains unchanged. In automotive maintenance instructions, this pattern often appears when an action phrase turns an instruction into its procedural counterpart. The entities, modifiers, and surrounding context remain largely invariant, while the action phrase determines the procedural relation. We define this task as Complementary Action Modeling (CAM). Given a maintenance instruction, the goal is to identify or generate its procedural counterpart by modifying the action phrase while preserving the remaining sentence context. This task focuses on three aspects: distinguishing complementarity from surface similarity, controlling generation at the action-phrase level, and evaluating relational correctness using retrieval, overlap-based, and human evaluation. Using a German automotive maintenance dataset, we examine these questions through candidate matching and controlled Seq2Seq generation. The results show that complementary maintenance instructions are best modeled as procedural associations grounded in subtle lexical cues. They should therefore not be treated as ordinary cases of sentence similarity or synonym-based paraphrasing.

In this paper, we systematically study how temporal metadata can be structurally embedded into NER models using a range of lightweight fusion strategies. We experiment with both absolute and relative temporal representations, injected into Transformer-based architectures via early or late fusion mechanisms such as cross-attention, adapters, and concatenation. ### [118] [Triadic Werewolf: A Jester Role for Multi-Hop Theory of Mind in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27909)
*Avni Mittal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入第三方角色‘小丑’扩展了狼人杀游戏，以测试大语言模型在三元激励结构下的多智能体推理能力。实验发现，传统二元社会推断任务无法揭示模型的真实心理建模能力，而引入反向激励的小丑角色使模型必须跨多个对立利益进行推理。在多款模型中，小丑获胜率高达60-70%，而狼人从未超过20%；GPT-4.1甚至在第一天就频繁投票淘汰小丑，这是一种自损行为。自我学习机制对DeepSeek和Llama有帮助，但损害了GPT-4.1的表现，且代价由村民承担而非狼人。只有DeepSeek学会了‘看似可疑但不刻意可疑’的微妙策略，并从中获益最多。该设计揭示了二元推理任务所隐藏的深层多智能体推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论心智评估多依赖二元社会推断游戏，其中每个线索仅指向单一隐藏方，导致模型可通过语言先验得分，而无需真正模拟对手动机。为更真实地检验模型的多智能体推理能力，需引入复杂激励结构，迫使模型进行跨主体利益权衡。

Method: 将狼人杀游戏扩展为包含小丑（第三方）的三元博弈：小丑赢在被投票出局，其效用与他人怀疑直接相反。通过60轮游戏测试GPT-4.1、DeepSeek-V3.1和Llama-3.3-70B在开启/关闭小丑自我学习条件下的表现，分析各角色胜率、投票行为及策略演化。

Result: 小丑在所有模型中均获得60-70%胜率，狼人胜率不超过20%；GPT-4.1在首日投票淘汰小丑的比例达60-70%，属于自损行为；自我学习对DeepSeek和Llama提升显著，但削弱GPT-4.1表现，且负面影响落在村民身上；仅DeepSeek发展出‘伪装可疑但不显故意’的高阶策略并最大化收益。

Conclusion: 三元激励结构能有效暴露大语言模型在多智能体推理中的真实能力，远超传统二元推理任务所能检测的范围。当前模型在复杂社会动态中仍存在策略短视与反向激励误判问题，表明其理论心智尚不健全。未来评估应引入更复杂的多主体博弈环境。

Abstract: Theory-of-mind evaluations of large language models typically use dyadic social-deduction games, where every observable cue points to a single hidden side, so a model with strong language priors can score well without ever simulating opponents' incentives. We extend the Werewolf game with a Jester, a third faction whose utility on peer suspicion is inverted because it wins by being voted out, so optimal play requires reasoning across three opposing utility functions. Across 60 games on GPT-4.1, DeepSeek-V3.1, and Llama-3.3-70B with Jester self-learning on and off, the Jester wins 60-70% of games while Werewolves never exceed 20%, and GPT-4.1 wolves vote the Jester out on day 1 in 60-70% of games, a strictly self-defeating action. Self-learning helps DeepSeek and Llama but hurts GPT-4.1, with the cost landing on Villagers rather than Werewolves. Only DeepSeek learns the subtle strategy of looking suspicious without looking intentionally suspicious, and it gains the most from the loop. Triadic incentive structure exposes a layer of multi-agent reasoning that dyadic deduction games leave invisible.

### [119] [VASAE: Naming SAE Dictionary Directions with Vocabulary-Aligned Anchoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27941)
*Kairui Zhang,Ziwen Yu,Zahraa S. Abdallah,Martha Lewis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: VASAE是一种新型稀疏自编码器方法，通过词汇对齐锚定训练，使每个特征直接关联到一个内在的词元名称（即与该特征最接近的词元嵌入对应的词元字符串），从而实现特征与词汇表的自然对应。在GPT-2-small和Llama-3.1-8B模型中，其在浅层和中层表现出高达90%以上的特征对齐率，且去除句子均值后仍能保留与输入上下文相关的语义信息，表明该方法可在训练阶段就建立特征与词元之间的语义联系，优于传统的后验命名方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稀疏自编码器（SAE）学习的特征通常缺乏与模型词元词汇的直接语义关联，需人工后验命名，导致解释性受限。本文旨在通过引入词汇对齐锚定机制，在训练过程中将学习到的特征与具体的词元字符串建立内在联系，提升特征的可解释性和语义连贯性。

Method: 提出词汇对齐稀疏自编码器（VASAE），在训练过程中施加词汇对齐约束，使得每个稀疏特征向量尽可能靠近某个词元嵌入；并通过计算最近邻词元嵌入来为每个特征分配一个内在的词元名称。同时采用句级均值减除以增强特征的上下文敏感性。

Result: 在GPT-2-small的前10层中，约90%的特征在0.8对齐阈值下实现了与词元的高精度匹配；在Llama-3.1-8B中，浅层特征对齐率达92.8%，而最终层对齐度较低。去除平均稀疏码后，剩余特征仍能反映附近输入词元的相关语义，验证了特征的上下文相关性。

Conclusion: 词汇对齐锚定能够有效引导稀疏自编码器在训练阶段将学到的特征与词元词汇建立内在联系，显著提升了特征的可解释性，为理解大模型内部表示提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) provide useful decompositions of Transformer residual streams, but their learned features are usually named post hoc rather than directly connected to the Transformer's token vocabulary. We introduce Vocabulary-Aligned Sparse Autoencoder (VASAE), a method that trains SAE features under vocabulary-aligned anchoring and assigns each feature an intrinsic token name: the token string whose embedding is nearest to that feature. Without reducing reconstruction quality compared with a standard SAE, VASAE produces dictionaries with vocabulary-aligned features. Using a 0.8 cutoff on the nearest-token alignment score, dictionaries trained on GPT-2-small post-residual streams align about 90% of features in layers 0--10. In Llama-3.1-8B, representative shallow and middle-layer dictionaries contain strongly aligned features, including 92.8% in the shallow layer, while the representative final-layer dictionary shows limited alignment. After subtracting the sentence-level mean sparse code, case studies show that many remaining intrinsic token names are relevant to nearby input tokens. These results suggest that vocabulary-aligned anchoring can connect learned features to intrinsic token names during training, complementing post hoc interpretation of learned dictionaries.

### [120] [An Empirical Analysis of Factual Errors in Human-Written Text and its Application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27959)
*Kazuma Iwamoto,Kazumasa Omura,Shotaro Ishihara*

Main category: cs.CL

Abstract: Factual Error Detection (FED), which is the task of identifying factually incorrect spans in a given text, has long been recognized as an important research problem. However, with the rapid rise of large language models (LLMs), research attention has shifted toward factual errors specific to LLM-generated text (hallucinations) and their detection. As a result, the detection of factual errors in human-written text has been relatively neglected. To address this gap, we first distill a taxonomy of human-induced factual errors by analyzing corrections of newspaper articles, a representative source of text that is guaranteed to be human-written and contains few grammatical errors. Our analysis revealed that there are characteristic categories such as kanji misconversions and numeral classifier errors, which are not focused in existing hallucination benchmarks. Based on the taxonomy, we then evaluate the FED capability of vanilla LLMs on synthesized realistic test cases and real corrections. Experimental results demonstrated that even high-performance LLMs such as GPT-5.4 achieved only word-level F1 score of 52% on the synthetic evaluation data, highlighting the task difficulty. Furthermore, a detailed analysis by detection difficulty revealed the current state of FED.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个从黑箱模型输出到临床叙事的可解释桥梁，显著提升了语音认知障碍检测系统的透明度与可信度，为未来智能化临床辅助诊断提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Speech-based cognitive impairment detection offers a noninvasive, accessible alternative to costly biomarker assays, yet transformer-based models remain clinically uninterpretable. TL;DR: ToxiREX is a multilingual, contextual dataset of Reddit comments annotated for implicit and context-dependent toxicity using a systematic toxic reasoning schema. It includes six languages and data from major events like the 2023 Turkey earthquakes and the Russian invasion of Ukraine. The dataset contains 125k training comments (LLM-annotated) and ~3k test comments (native speaker-annotated), with strong evidence that annotation disagreements reflect valid interpretations rather than noise. Baseline models show room for improvement, highlighting the task's difficulty. ToxiREX enables evaluation of hierarchical, schema-based toxicity detection across languages and contexts.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing toxicity detection datasets often fail to capture implicit, context-dependent, and multilingual aspects of toxic language. This work aims to address these gaps by introducing a structured, multilingual dataset grounded in a robust toxic reasoning schema that supports nuanced, explainable annotations.

Method: The authors developed a toxic reasoning schema based on prior work, applied it to Reddit comment threads related to real-world events, and collected multilingual data across English, Arabic, Turkish, Spanish, German, and Dutch. They performed context-preserving preprocessing, created a large training set via LLM annotation, and curated a smaller test set with native speaker annotations. Evaluation strategies were designed for hierarchical, schema-based predictions.

Result: Models perform better than random but still have significant room for improvement, indicating the complexity of detecting implicit and context-dependent toxicity. Annotation disagreements are largely defensible, suggesting interpretive diversity rather than noise. The dataset enables new benchmarks for multilingual, contextual, and schema-driven toxicity analysis.

Conclusion: ToxiREX is the first dataset to combine multilingualism, conversational context, implicit toxicity, and structured schema-based annotations. It sets a new standard for evaluating AI systems in detecting nuanced, context-sensitive toxicity, with clear potential for advancing responsible NLP research.

Abstract: We introduce a new, contextual, multilingual dataset called ToxiREX: Toxic REasoning in ConteXt. The dataset consists of threads of Reddit comments and structured characterizations of what the comments imply, following a systematic toxic reasoning schema developed in a previous paper. Using the schema allows us to capture and explain implicit and context-dependent toxicity, while supporting mappings to existing toxicity taxonomies. The dataset includes comments in six languages (English, Arabic, Turkish, Spanish, German, and Dutch), collected from posts connected to specific major events (e.g. the 2023 Turkey earthquakes; the Russian invasion of Ukraine). We describe the context-preserving preprocessing of the threads. We create a training set of 125 thousand comments which is annotated by a commercially available LLM, and a test set of just under three thousand comments that is annotated by native speakers. We show that apparent disagreements in the test set annotations often reflect defensible alternative interpretations rather than noise. Finally, we provide baseline results by prompting and fine-tuning language models. To produce these results, we develop evaluation strategies for our hierarchical, schema-based predictions. While models perform better than random, there remains a lot of room for improvement, showing the task to be challenging. ToxiREX is the first dataset to simultaneously incorporate multiple languages, conversational context, and implicit toxicity, while using the toxic reasoning schema for rich, structured annotations. Dataset available at: https://github.com/cltl/toxirex

### [124] [The Signal-Coverage Matrix: Stratifying Type and Semantic Errors in Statement Autoformalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28013)
*Chengxiao Dai,Zhaokun Yan,Zhanhui Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出信号覆盖矩阵，通过交叉检查Lean归约器（成功/失败）与语义等价性判断（等价/不等价），将LLM自动形式化输出分为四类：真成功（TS）、仅类型正确（TO）、仅语义正确（SO）、两者均失败（BF）。在ProofNet#和MiniF2F-test上，使用DeepSeek V4-Pro对比Vanilla、Lean-Retry、Sample-Filter和分层自动形式化（SAF）方法发现：(1) 三种归约反馈方法使TS提升34%-36%，其中约64%为类型层面恢复，而SO净变化基本不变（87.5%原语义错误被修复，新增8个）；(2) 各方法的TO转TS率为23/61（95%置信区间[26.6%, 50.3%]），该比率可预测未见方法的ΔTS，误差仅2/186，且ΔTC与Vanilla归约失败率呈高度线性关系（R²=0.96）；(3) 两位评审者对归约反馈输出的分歧达26-37个百分点（远高于Vanilla的7个百分点），其中30-56%的符号判断假阴性源于归约器强制重写。残余错误最终减少至两个金标准形式化错误。因此，应根据具体细胞转移来归因TC%提升，而非仅依赖单一指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有头类型正确率（TC%）指标虽从约53%升至76%，但无法揭示不同方法解决的具体错误类型。为更精细评估自动形式化方法的改进，需区分类型错误与语义错误的修复情况，避免误判提升来源。

Method: 提出信号覆盖矩阵，结合Lean归约器结果与语义等价性判断，将输出分类为四类：真成功（TS）、仅类型正确（TO）、仅语义正确（SO）、两者均失败（BF）。通过在ProofNet#和MiniF2F-test上对比多种方法（Vanilla、Lean-Retry、Sample-Filter、SAF），分析各细胞间的转移模式，并利用统计建模预测性能提升。

Result: 三种归约反馈方法带来34%-36%的TS提升，主要源于64%的类型层面恢复；语义层面修复几乎无净增益（87.5%原错误被救回，新增8个）；TO转TS率稳定在23/61，具有强预测能力（ΔTS误差小，ΔTC与归约失败率高度线性，R²=0.96）；评审分歧显著增大，部分假阴性源于归约器强制重写；最终残余错误降至两个金标准形式化错误。

Conclusion: TC%的提升应基于其背后具体错误类型的修复路径进行解释，不能仅依赖整体指标。信号覆盖矩阵能有效揭示不同方法的真实贡献，强调应以细胞间转移为基础评估自动形式化进展。

Abstract: Headline type-correctness (TC\%) of LLM autoformalization has climbed from $\sim$53\% to $\sim$76\% in two years, yet this scalar conceals which errors each method resolves. We propose a signal-coverage matrix that crosses the Lean elaborator (pass/fail) with a semantic-equivalence judgment (equivalent/not), sorting every output into one of four cells: true success (TS), type-only (TO), semantic-only (SO), or both fail (BF). On ProofNet\# and MiniF2F-test with DeepSeek V4-Pro across Vanilla, Lean-Retry, Sample-Filter, and Stratified Autoformalization (SAF): (1) the +34 to +36 TS gain across the three elab-feedback methods is $\sim$64\% type-stratum recovery, with SO flat on net (87.5\% of original semantic errors rescued, 8 newly created). (2) The TO-to-TS rate is 23/61 for each method (Wilson 95\% CI [26.6\%, 50.3\%]), and this stratum-level recovery rate predicts $Δ$TS on held-out methods to within 2/186 and renders $Δ$TC linear in the Vanilla elab-fail rate across six (model, dataset) cells ($R^2=0.96$). (3) The two judges disagree by 26 to 37 pp on elab-feedback outputs (vs. 7 pp on Vanilla), with 30 to 56\% of symbolic-judge false negatives traceable to elaborator-forced rewrites. The persistent residual reduces to two gold-formalization errors. TC\% gains should be credited by which cell moved, not by the scalar alone.

### [126] [Can LLMs Judge Better Than They Generate? Evaluating Task Asymmetry, Mechanistic Interpretability and Transferability for In-Context QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28050)
*Sambaran Bandyopadhyay*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究检验了LLM-as-a-Judge和自评估流水线中隐含的假设——评估比生成更容易。在受控的上下文问答设置中，发现评估并不总是更简单：在四个基准测试中的三个上，生成准确率高于自评估，仅多跳推理的MuSiQue例外。注意力分析显示，评估过程对上下文的关注度仅为生成的3-5倍，且几乎不读取候选答案。通过LoRA微调验证，这种不对称性并非训练造成的。生成微调导致过度接受错误答案，而评估微调则损害了生成质量。研究结果挑战了自评估流水线的核心假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自评估流水线依赖于评估比生成更简单的假设，但这一假设在真实场景中缺乏实证支持，尤其是在排除参数知识干扰的受控设置下。本文旨在检验该假设的有效性，并揭示其潜在缺陷。

Method: 在四个基准数据集（SQuAD 2.0、DROP、HotpotQA、MuSiQue）上，使用两个模型进行受控的上下文问答实验，让模型对自己生成的答案进行自评估。通过注意力机制分析评估与生成过程的差异，并采用LoRA微调验证不对称性的稳定性。

Result: 在三个数据集上，生成的准确率高于自评估；评估过程对上下文和候选答案的关注度显著低于生成过程；微调实验表明，生成和评估能力之间的不对称性是固有的，而非训练偏差。

Conclusion: 评估并不总是比生成更容易，当前自评估流水线所依赖的核心假设可能不成立。这提示需重新审视基于大模型的自动评估方法的设计逻辑，特别是在复杂推理任务中。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge and self-evaluation pipelines implicitly assume that evaluation is easier than generation. We test this in a controlled in-context QA setting where a context passage is the sole information source and each model judges the answer it generated, removing the parametric-knowledge confound of open-domain comparisons. Across four benchmarks (SQuAD 2.0, DROP, HotpotQA, MuSiQue) and two models, evaluation is not uniformly easier: generation accuracy exceeds self-evaluation on three of four, with multi-hop MuSiQue the exception. Attention analysis reveals why: evaluation attends to context 3--5x less than generation does and barely reads the candidate answer. LoRA fine-tuning confirms the asymmetry is not a training artifact: generation fine-tuning induces over-acceptance and evaluation fine-tuning degrades generation. These findings challenge core assumptions in self-evaluation pipelines.

### [127] [MultiHashFormer: Hash-based Generative Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28057)
*Huiyin Xue,Atsuki Yamaguchi,Nikolaos Aletras*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MultiHashFormer 是一种基于哈希的新型语言模型框架，通过多个独立哈希函数将每个词元映射为唯一的哈希签名（短序列的离散哈希ID），实现参数高效的自回归生成。该方法在编码器中压缩哈希签名，在解码器中生成下个词元的哈希签名并还原为文本，克服了传统哈希方法在因果语言模型中的限制。在100M、1B和3B参数规模下均优于标准Transformer模型，并能以恒定参数量支持多语言词汇扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于哈希的方法虽可减少参数量，但因多对一哈希碰撞无法用于因果语言模型。本文旨在设计一种支持哈希自回归的架构，兼顾参数效率与生成能力。

Method: 提出MultiHashFormer框架：使用多个独立哈希函数生成唯一哈希签名；通过哈希编码器压缩签名至潜向量；利用哈希解码器生成下一个词元的哈希签名并映射回文本；结合Transformer解码器完成自回归生成。

Result: 在100M、1B和3B参数规模下，MultiHashFormer在多个基准测试中表现优于标准Transformer模型；且在多语言词汇扩展场景中保持恒定参数量，无需修改。

Conclusion: MultiHashFormer成功实现了参数高效的哈希自回归，兼具高性能与可扩展性，为大规模语言模型的轻量化设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) represent tokens using embedding matrices that scale linearly with the vocabulary size. To constrain the parameter footprint, prior work proposes hashing many tokens into a single vector within encoder-only models. While this offers parameter efficiency, many-to-one collisions prevent its use in causal LMs. In this paper, we propose MultiHashFormer, a new framework that allows hash-based autoregression. Each token is represented as a unique hash signature, a short sequence of discrete hash IDs, generated by multiple independent hash functions. A Hash Encoder compresses this signature into a single latent vector for processing by a Transformer decoder. Then, a Hash Decoder generates the hash signature of the next token, which is then mapped back to text. We evaluate our approach at the 100M, 1B and 3B parameter scales, demonstrating that MultiHashFormer consistently outperforms standard Transformer LMs across multiple benchmarks. Furthermore, we show that our model handles multilingual vocabulary expansion with a constant parameter footprint without any modifications.

</details>


### [128] [Mechanism-Driven Monitors for Preemptive Detection of LLM Training Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28116)
*Ruixuan Huang,Yipei Wang,Wenyi Fang,Hantao Huang,Yifan Huang,Ansheng You,Zhenxing Zhang,Shuai Wang,Fan Wu,Yang Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大规模语言模型训练中的稳定性故障检测，提出通过关键模块的功能机制设计内部监控器，以在损失崩溃前数千步内提前发现异常。针对低精度Flash Attention，通过监测QK双线性分解的谱熵变化来捕捉早期异常；对于MoE路由器，则基于其专家选择功能设计指标。实验表明，这些信号对不同故障类型具有显著区分性，可提前预警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模语言模型训练依赖大量加速器和长时间计算，一旦出现数值或超参数故障，可能导致训练动态失稳，且在损失和梯度范数仍正常的情况下持续数千步，造成巨大损失。因此亟需在早期阶段检测训练不稳定性。

Method: 从关键模块的功能角色出发，分析其最早可能出现故障信号的计算位置，构建机制驱动的内部监控器。具体包括：1）对低精度Flash Attention，监测QK双线性分解的谱熵；2）对MoE路由器，基于其在专家选择中的作用设计评估指标。

Result: 在低精度注意力、大学习率及复合故障的故障注入实验中，所提监控信号能有效区分不同类型的故障，并在损失发散前数千步即触发预警，表现出良好的早期检测能力。

Conclusion: 通过基于功能机制的内部监控设计，能够实现对训练不稳定性的早期、精准检测，显著提升大规模模型训练的鲁棒性与效率。

Abstract: Frontier large language model training consumes massive accelerator fleets and long wall-clock computation, making stability failures costly when they occur. After a numerical or a hyperparameter fault has already destabilized the training dynamics, it may continue for thousands of steps while loss and gradient norms still appear normal. We study mechanism-driven detection of training instability by deriving internal monitors from the functional role of each critical module and from the earliest computational sites where failures are expected to produce measurable signatures. For low-precision flash attention, we monitor the spectral entropy of a QK bilinear decomposition, whose first-order term becomes abnormal before the loss fully collapses. For MoE routers, we derive indicators from their role in expert selection. Our fault-injection experiments on low-precision attention, large learning-rate, and combined faults show that these signals provide distinct signatures for different failures, triggering thousands of steps before loss divergence.

</details>


### [129] [From Tokens to States: LLMs as a Special Case of World Models and the Continuous Path Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28127)
*Paul Dubois*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了大语言模型（LLMs）与世界模型之间的二元对立观点，提出LLMs实际上是世界模型的一种退化特例。通过将状态空间定义为所有可能的标记序列，并将唯一动作设为添加一个标记，作者表明世界模型是对LLMs的严格推广而非替代。此外，论文指出从自回归标记预测（NTP）到联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）之间存在一条连续谱系，包括多标记预测、未来摘要预测和下一潜在状态预测等中间阶段。沿着这一谱系逐步放松LLM的约束，也相应地放弃了其两大可扩展训练优势：互联网规模的自监督数据和为离散标记预测设计的Transformer架构。论文进一步将这两个问题作为开放研究课题进行探讨，即如何从自监督文本过渡到带标注行为的环境数据，以及Transformer是否能泛化到连续状态预测，或需要新的基础构件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI社区普遍将大语言模型（LLMs）与世界模型视为相互对立的技术路径，这种二元划分限制了对通用智能实现路径的深入理解。作者旨在打破这一僵化框架，揭示两者之间的内在连续性，推动更系统、更连贯的智能模型发展。

Method: 通过形式化分析LLMs与世界模型在状态空间、动作空间和动态演化机制上的对应关系，论证LLMs是世界模型在特定约束下的退化形式；构建从自回归标记预测到未来潜变量预测的连续谱系，识别现有研究中的中间阶段；对数据来源与模型架构的可扩展性进行理论反思，提出两个关键开放问题。

Result: 证明了世界模型是对LLMs的严格推广，而非替代；揭示了从传统LLM到高级世界模型的连续演进路径；指出了在数据与架构层面面临的重大挑战，为后续研究提供方向。

Conclusion: LLMs并非独立于世界模型的存在，而是其特殊情形。未来的发展应聚焦于探索连续谱系中的中间形态，同时解决自监督数据向真实环境数据转化及模型架构适应连续状态预测的核心难题。

Abstract: The AI community has framed the relationship between large language models (LLMs) and world models as a dichotomy: LLMs predict tokens; world models simulate reality. Yann LeCun argues in 2022 that reaching general intelligence requires abandoning autoregressive token prediction in favour of latent-space architectures. This framing is unnecessarily binary. Two claims will be defended. First, LLMs are a degenerate special case of world models: the state space is the set of all token sequences, the only action is appending one token, and world models are therefore a strict generalisation of LLMs, not a replacement. Second, there is a natural continuous spectrum from NTP to JEPA, with multi-token prediction, future-summary prediction, and next-latent prediction as intermediate stations already populated by current research. Moving along this spectrum relaxes the LLM constraints one by one. It also progressively surrenders the two practical advantages that make LLMs trainable at scale: internet-scale self-supervised data, and a transformer architecture co-designed for discrete token prediction. Both are examined as open research questions: the data question (the cliff from self-supervised text to instrumented action-labelled environments) and the architecture question (whether the transformer generalises to continuous-state prediction, or whether a new primitive is needed).

</details>


### [130] [Cognitive Episodes in LLM Reasoning Traces Enable Interpretable Human Item Difficulty Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28186)
*Chenguang Wang,Ming Li,Xinyue Zeng,Zhuochun Li,Hong Jiao,Tianyi Zhou,Dawei Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Epi2Diff 是一种新框架，通过将大推理模型（LRM）的推理轨迹转化为认知上合理的“事件序列”，来预测人类对题目难度的感知。该方法结合了推理过程中的动态特征与题目的语义表示，显著优于现有基线方法，在多个真实数据集上表现优异，尤其在SAT衍生的分类任务中相对提升达8.1%。分析显示，更难题目引发更费力、迭代性强且以实现为中心的推理动态，而非仅仅更长的回答。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有题目难度预测方法依赖昂贵的人工校准或仅基于文本的特征，缺乏对认知过程的理解。本文旨在通过大推理模型的推理轨迹，揭示题目带来的问题解决负担，从而提供更具解释性的难度预测方式。

Method: Epi2Diff 将 LRM 的推理轨迹分解为功能性的认知事件序列，提取反映推理规模、努力分配和状态转换的动态特征，并融合语义表示用于难度预测。

Result: 在四个真实世界的人类难度数据集上，Epi2Diff 均显著优于多种强基线方法，包括微调的小型语言模型、LLM 的上下文学习以及监督式微调。在 SAT 衍生的分类任务中，平均相对性能提升 8.1%。进一步分析表明，高难度题目引发更复杂、迭代性更强的推理行为。

Conclusion: Epi2Diff 证明了大模型推理轨迹中的认知事件序列可作为预测人类题目难度的可解释、高预测力的过程表征，为教育测量提供了基于推理模型的新视角。

Abstract: Predicting human item difficulty is central to educational assessment, where reliable estimates support fairness and effective test construction. Existing methods often depend on costly human calibration or item-level textual representations, providing limited evidence about the cognitive processes that make items difficult. We argue that difficulty should be viewed not only as a property of item text, but also as an observable consequence of the problem-solving burden an item induces. Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) offer scalable process evidence through reasoning traces, but such evidence must be structured to support interpretable modeling. To this end, we introduce Epi2Diff (Episode to Difficulty), a framework that maps LRM reasoning traces into cognitively grounded episode sequences. These episodes group trace segments into functional problem-solving states, enabling difficulty to be modeled through reasoning scale, effort allocation, and state transitions. Epi2Diff extracts compact episode-dynamic features and combines them with semantic item representations for human difficulty prediction. Experiments on four real-world human difficulty datasets show that Epi2Diff consistently outperforms strong baselines, including fine-tuned small language models, LLM in-context learning, and supervised LLM adaptation. On SAT-derived classification benchmarks, Epi2Diff achieves an 8.1% average relative gain over supervised LLM fine-tuning baselines. Further analyses show that harder items induce more effortful, iterative, and implementation-centered episode dynamics, rather than merely longer responses. These results demonstrate that cognitive episodes in LRM reasoning traces provide a predictive and interpretable process representation for human item difficulty, offering a new lens for educational measurement with reasoning models.

</details>


### [131] [Vision-Default, Prior-Override: Causal Mechanisms of Perception-Knowledge Conflict in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28273)
*Niclas Lietzow,Danielle Bitterman,Carsten Eickhoff,William Rudman,Michal Golovanevsky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过激活修补和组件消融分析，揭示了视觉-语言模型（VLM）在感知与知识冲突时的因果机制。发现视觉接地是默认行为，而先验知识依赖于网络后半部分少数关键注意力头（2.5-4.8%），这些头负责将存储的世界知识映射到输出。移除这些头可使68-96%的知识导向预测转向视觉导向，但对视觉导向预测影响极小（0.8-7.5%），表明存在不对称因果结构。这些头分为路由头和写入头，构成跨模型家族和规模一致的稀疏因果回路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解视觉-语言模型在视觉证据与记忆知识冲突时如何决策，现有研究缺乏组件级因果解释，亟需揭示其内在机制以提升系统可靠性。

Method: 结合多粒度激活修补（残差流、注意力头、MLP子层）与模型组件消融，辅以机械分析，评估不同组件在感知-知识冲突中的作用。

Result: 识别出少量关键注意力头（2.5-4.8%）集中于网络后半部分，对知识驱动回答起因果必要作用；移除它们可显著改变知识导向预测，但对视觉导向影响微弱，揭示不对称因果结构；这些头分解为路由头与写入头，形成跨模型一致的稀疏因果电路。

Conclusion: 视觉-语言模型中感知与知识的冲突由一个稀疏、可定位的因果电路调控，其中少数注意力头主导知识注入，该结构具有普遍性且不受模型规模影响，为理解并改进多模态系统可靠性提供了机制基础。

Abstract: Vision-language models must reconcile visual evidence with memorized world knowledge when the two conflict. How they resolve this conflict shapes the reliability of multimodal systems, yet prior work characterizes it behaviorally without a component-level causal account. We combine activation patching across three granularities (residual stream, attention heads, and MLP sublayers) with model-component ablation studies and mechanistic analysis. Across three VLM families, we find that visual grounding emerges by default, whereas prior grounding depends on a small set of causally necessary attention heads (2.5-4.8%) concentrated in the second half of the network. These heads enable answers from stored world knowledge (e.g., "red" for a strawberry) despite conflicting visual input. Ablating them flips predictions from knowledge-grounded to visually grounded answers in 68-96% of cases under prior-knowledge prompts, but changes only 0.8-7.5% of visually grounded predictions, establishing an asymmetric causal structure. The identified heads decompose into routing heads, which modulate information flow, and writing heads, which directly project answer tokens into the residual stream. This structure is consistent across model families and scales, revealing a sparse causal circuit underlying perception-knowledge conflict in VLMs.

</details>

### [132] [AI-Model Network: Concept, Current State and Future](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27382)

Method: 提出AI-ModelNet概念，设计分层系统架构，构建原型系统，通过多样化应用案例验证其可行性，结合理论分析与实证测试推进技术落地。

Result: 成功构建了支持模型互联、能力共享与协同推理的原型系统，验证了AI-ModelNet在实际场景中的可行性与有效性，为大模型生态的协同发展提供了新路径。

Conclusion: AI-ModelNet作为一种新型人工智能模型互联范式，有望突破当前大模型应用的瓶颈，推动形成开放、协同、高效的智能生态体系，是迈向通用人工智能的重要一步。

Abstract: While the primary function of computers lies in computation and processing, the core value of the Internet is rooted in sharing and collaboration. Computers create the Internet, and the Internet empowers the value of computers. The rapid development of the Internet, cloud computing, and big data is pushing artificial intelligence into the era of large models (LMs). However, the practical application of LMs is currently hindered by high training costs and deployment complexities, driving a shift toward lightweight, private, and domain-specific models. With the rapid proliferation and wide distribution of heterogeneous models, enabling effective interaction and collaboration among them has emerged as a critical bottleneck that urgently needs to be addressed in LM development. Drawing inspiration from the development of the Internet, this paper proposes the concept, vision, and system architecture of world wide AI-model network (AI-ModelNet). It is a novel paradigm that achieves interconnection, capability sharing, and collaborative reasoning by establishing pathways between models. We first briefly review the current state of single-model and multi-model research. Subsequently, the systemic vision and hierarchical architecture of AI-ModelNet are articulated, followed by validation of the framework's feasibility through a prototype system and diverse application cases. Finally, key directions for future research are discussed preliminarily.

### [133] [When Does Personality Composition Matter for Multi-Agent LLM Teams?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27443)
*Aryan Keluskar,Amrita Bhattacharjee,Huan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了人格特质对大型语言模型在多智能体协作中任务表现的影响。通过在编码、开放式研究合作和竞争性谈判三种任务中操控人格特质，发现人格影响取决于任务结构：在编码任务中，低亲和性导致沟通方式显著变化但对任务完成影响较小；而在开放合作与谈判任务中，相同的人格操控会显著降低绩效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究显示，低亲和性提示会导致对抗性语言，高亲和性则促进合作，但人格风格与任务结果之间的关系尚未在多个领域系统考察。本研究旨在揭示人格组成是否影响多智能体团队的整体表现。

Method: 在三个不同任务领域（结构化编码、开放研究协作、竞争性谈判）中，对前沿大语言模型进行人格特质的操控实验，比较不同人格组合下的沟通行为与任务绩效。

Result: 在编码任务中，低亲和性引起明显沟通变化，但对里程碑完成影响有限；而在开放合作与谈判任务中，低亲和性显著降低任务表现。表明人格影响具有任务依赖性。

Conclusion: 人格特质对多智能体系统性能有重要影响，但其作用高度依赖于任务结构。设计多智能体系统时需考虑任务特性，不能简单依赖人格操控来优化表现。

Abstract: Personality prompting shapes how large language models communicate, yet whether these behavioral shifts affect objective task outcomes remains under-explored. Prior work shows that agents prompted with low agreeableness produce adversarial language, while those prompted with high agreeableness become cooperative, but the relationship between communication style and task performance has not been systematically examined across multiple domains. In this work, we investigate whether personality composition matters for multi-agent team performance by manipulating personality traits across frontier LLMs on three task domains: structured coding, open-ended research collaboration, and competitive bargaining. We find that personality effects depend critically on task structure. In coding tasks, low agreeableness leads to large communication shifts that have little effect on milestone completion. In open-ended collaboration and bargaining, the same manipulation substantially degrades performance. We discuss implications for multi-agent system design and the limits of personality manipulation.

</details>


### [134] [Internalizing the Future: A Unified Agentic Training Paradigm for World Model Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27483)
*Xuan Zhang,Zhijian Zhou,Lingfeng Qiao,Yulei Qin,Ke Li,Xing Sun,Xiaoyu Tan,Chao Qu,Yuan Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出通过训练单一自回归模型来实现大语言模型代理的前瞻性规划，使其能够生成未来状态推演和条件化成功预测，从而具备类似Q值的文本表示。针对现有方法在长程任务中仅表面模仿前瞻性的缺陷，作者设计了三阶段训练范式：(i) 世界模型代理中段训练（WM-AMT）注入潜在预测能力；(ii) 格式诱导监督微调（FE-SFT）结构化该能力；(iii) 前瞻条件强化学习（FC-RL）优化生成模拟的校准与实用性。实验表明，在搜索和数学推理任务中，该方法显著优于其他基线，证明了以能力为导向的训练流程对实现真实、校准的前瞻至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型代理在长程任务中仍为被动反应型，缺乏人类般的‘假设性’推理能力，无法在行动前评估多种可能计划的后果。因此需要引入内部世界模型，使模型具备对未来结果进行模拟与评估的能力。

Method: 提出三阶段训练框架：1. WM-AMT 在中段训练中注入潜藏的预测能力；2. FE-SFT 通过格式引导的方式显式结构化预测能力；3. FC-RL 利用前瞻性条件信号进行强化学习，提升模拟结果的准确性与实用性。

Result: 在搜索与数学推理任务上，所提方法持续优于各类训练基线，验证了其在生成真实、可信赖的未来推演方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 有效的内部世界建模需以能力构建为先，通过系统性训练流程实现真正接地且校准良好的前瞻性规划，而非仅表面模仿。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capability in sequential decision-making, yet they remains fundamentally reactive in long-horizon tasks. Unlike humans who employ "what-if" reasoning to evaluate potential plans before commitment, standard agents lack an internal world model to simulate future outcomes. Therefore, we propose to internalize future-aware planning by training a single autoregressive model to verbalize both a prospective state rollout and a plan-conditioned success estimate-a textual analogue of the Q-value. Crucially, we identify a format-capability gap: simply fine-tuning agents on look-ahead traces during post-training leads to superficial mimicry of foresight without genuine predictive grounding. To bridge this gap, we introduce a three-stage training paradigm: (i) World Model Agentic Mid-Training (WM-AMT) to inject latent predictive capabilities into the policy; (ii) Format-Eliciting SFT (FE-SFT) to structure this injected capability; and (iii) Foresight-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (FC-RL) to refine the calibration and utility of the generated simulations. Evaluated on search and mathematical reasoning tasks, our approach consistently outperforms other training baselines. Our results demonstrate that effective internal world modeling in LLM agents requires a capability-first training pipeline to achieve grounded and calibrated foresight.

</details>


### [135] [Odyssey: Constructing Verifiable Local Truth-Preserving Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27593)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ODYSSEY 是一个用于构建可验证、局部保真基础模型的范畴框架，通过组合称为"foundries"（工厂）的构建模块来实现。这些 foundries 定义了局部上下文、局部表示族、限制映射、粘合规则、障碍策略、更新义务和面向人类的视图。每个 foundry 是一个知识的有组织层叠，包含论证组件。具体 foundries 由通用 foundries（如证据/论证、操作决策、机构/财务、市场意义、科学挑战、研究计划、助手构建、评估工具等）构成。通用工厂学习（UFL）将 foundry 构建形式化为左和右 Kan 扩展的组合：左 Kan 扩展将局部工件滚动为候选 foundry，右 Kan 扩展则强制执行限制、粘合、障碍和论证条件以实现晋升。Foundry SQL（FSQL）是一种小型类型化查询界面，用于切片维护的 foundry 工件，并使用 TICKET（基于因果 Kan 扩展的拓扑集成）认证来接纳外部或预构建模型进入持久的 ODYSSEY 状态。该框架已在多种具体 foundries 中完全实现并测试，证明相同的范畴机制可支持领域构建、工件重放、层叠诊断、基于 Toulmin/局部大语言模型的审查、残差障碍账本以及跨异构来源的优化因果主张提取。本文将作为 ICML 2026 的 2.5 小时教程呈现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基础模型缺乏可验证性与局部保真性，难以在复杂、多源环境中可靠运行。需要一种系统性方法来构建可追溯、可审查、可组合的模型架构，确保知识的局部一致性与整体协调性。为此，提出一种基于范畴论的统一框架，以实现对模型构建过程的严格控制与透明管理。

Method: 采用范畴论中的层叠（sheaf）理论构建 ODYSSEY 框架，核心是定义 and 组合 foundries。通过左 Kan 扩展生成候选 foundry，右 Kan 扩展强制满足限制、粘合、障碍与论证条件。引入 UFL 形式化 foundry 构建流程，使用 FSQL 提供类型安全的查询接口，并通过 TICKET 认证机制整合外部模型，实现状态持久化与可信性保障。

Result: ODYSSEY 在多个具体 foundry 上成功实现并验证，展现出强大的通用性与可扩展性。能够支持领域构建、工件重放、层叠诊断、局部模型审查、残差障碍追踪及跨源因果主张提取。所有功能均由统一的范畴数学框架驱动，实现了从构造到验证的端到端可控性。

Conclusion: ODYSSEY 提供了一种基于范畴论的系统性方法，用于构建可验证、局部保真的基础模型。其核心在于将模型视为可组合的、带有论证结构的层叠对象，通过 UFL 和 FSQL 支持自动化构建与可信查询。该框架为未来可解释、可审计的人工智能系统奠定了理论与实践基础。

Abstract: We introduce a categorical framework called ODYSSEY for constructing verifiable, local truth-preserving foundation models as compositions of foundries: building-block architectural components that specify a cover of local contexts, local representation families, restriction maps, gluing rules, obstruction policies, update obligations, and human-facing views. A foundry is an organized sheaf of knowledge that carries within it an argumentation component. Concrete foundries are built from generic foundries such as evidence/argument, operational decision, institutional/financial, market meaning, scientific challenge, research-program, assistant-build, and evaluation-harness foundries. Universal Foundry Learning (UFL) formalizes foundry construction as a composition of left and right Kan extensions, with left Kan extension rolling local artifacts into candidate foundries and right Kan extension enforcing the restriction, gluing, obstruction, and argumentation conditions required for promotion. Foundry SQL (FSQL) is a small typed query surface for slicing maintained foundry artifacts that uses TICKET (Topos Integration using Causal Kan Extension Transformers) certification for admitting external or pre-built models into durable ODYSSEY state. ODYSSEY is fully implemented and tested across a wide spectrum of concrete foundries, showing that the same categorical machinery supports domain construction, artifact replay, sheaf diagnostics, grounded Toulmin/local-LLM scrutiny, residual-obstruction ledgers, and optimized TICKET-compatible causal-claim extraction across heterogeneous sources. This paper is to be presented as a 2.5 hour tutorial at ICML 2026. The tutorial home page is at https://bit.ly/4ajS0nA.

</details>


### [136] [DysLexLens: A Low-Resource LLM Framework for Analysing Dyslexic Learners Insights from Online Forums](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27619)

Motivation: 当前尽管阅读障碍学习者越来越多地使用 AI 工具辅助读写和学习，但其真实使用体验仍缺乏系统研究，尤其在低资源论坛环境中。现有方法难以有效处理噪声数据并保证生成内容的可信度。因此需要一种可追溯、可验证且适用于非专业语境的分析框架。

Method: 提出 DysLexLens 框架，包含四部分：1）利用词典驱动方法从社交媒体中筛选出与阅读障碍和 AI 相关的高质量帖子；2）结合大语言模型与知识图谱进行语义分析与问题推理；3）采用 RAGAS 和查询鲁棒性等量化指标评估响应性能；4）制定结构化定性评估标准，重点检测幻觉与证据一致性。

Result: 在 Reddit 的阅读障碍相关论坛数据上，使用 30 个问题测试表明，DysLexLens 能有效提取有意义模式，生成可验证的回答，并实现高精度的响应质量评估。框架展现出良好的泛化能力，适用于其他低资源论坛场景。所有样本数据、问题及评估结果均已公开于 GitHub，支持复现。

Abstract: Dyslexic learners increasingly use artificial intelligence (AI) tools to support reading, writing, organisation, and study-related tasks. However, their lived experiences with these tools remain largely underexamined. This paper proposes DysLexLens, a low-resource LLM framework, designed to analyse dyslexic learners experience with AI through online forum discussions. DysLexLens is designed as an end-to-end, evidence-traceable architecture which transforms noisy social media posts into a dictionary-driven corpora, provides knowledge-graph (KG)-based question reasoning, generates verifiable query responses, and enables response evaluation through quantitative and human-grounded assessment. DysLexLens has four key features. First, it employs a dictionary-driven filtering method to construct a more focused Reddit corpus on dyslexia and AI, filtering out noisy and weakly related posts to improve the relevance of data collected from low-resource forum contexts. Second, it integrates LLM-assisted semantic analysis with KG-based query reasoning to uncover meaningful patterns. Third, it has quantitative evaluation metrics (RAGAS and Query Robustness) to measure LLM-generated response performance. Fourth, it provides structured qualitative validation guidelines for assessing response quality, with a specific focus on hallucination and evidence alignment. We demonstrate the effectiveness of DysLexLens using dyslexia-related Reddit forum data and 30 questions. The results show its potential generalisability to other low-resource forum data contexts. DysLexLens, sample data, questions and evaluation results are available at Github to support reproducibility.

### [137] [MER-R1: Multimodal Emotion Reasoning via Slow-Fast Thinking Synergy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27652)
*Zhiyuan Han,Beier Zhu,Wenwen Tong,Chengwei Qin,Xinyi Wang,Jiayu Zhang,Jiangnan Chen,Hewei Guo,Dongchuan Ran,Lewei Lu,Xun Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究发现，显式推理并不一定提升多模态情感识别（MER）的准确率，尽管它使预测更具可解释性。快速思维（直接回答）往往优于经过深思熟虑的慢思维。快思维提高召回率，产生更广泛且自信的预测；慢思维则通过保守过滤错误类别提升精确率。为此，作者提出MER-R1框架，通过强化学习将快慢思维的互补性显式优化。双目标解耦分离召回与精确率作为独立优化信号，实现联合优化而非权衡。慢-快思维置信度校准使最终慢思维结果与快思维直觉一致，增强正确情感、抑制错误情感。理论分析表明该协同机制可缓解优化中的方差干扰。在MER-UniBench和MME-Emotion数据集上，MER-R1达到当前最优性能，并真正使推理助力情感识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管显式推理能提升预测可解释性，但其对多模态情感识别（MER）准确率的提升效果不明确，甚至可能不如直接快速回答。现有方法常在召回率与精确率之间进行权衡，缺乏有效整合快慢思维优势的机制。因此，亟需一种能够显式融合快思维（高召回）与慢思维（高精确）互补性的优化框架，以真正发挥推理在情感识别中的作用。

Method: 提出MER-R1框架，采用强化学习实现快慢思维的互补优化。通过双目标解耦，将召回率与精确率分别建模为独立优化信号，避免传统权衡。引入慢-快思维置信度校准机制，使慢思维输出与快思维直觉对齐，从而增强正确情感判断并抑制错误分类。同时提供理论支持，证明该协同机制可降低优化过程中的方差干扰。

Result: 在MER-UniBench和MME-Emotion两个基准数据集上，MER-R1均取得当前最优性能。实验验证了快慢思维互补性确实可被有效利用，且推理不仅提升了可解释性，也真正提高了情感识别的准确性。

Conclusion: 显式推理若设计得当，可显著提升多模态情感识别性能。通过将快思维的高召回与慢思维的高精确通过双目标解耦与置信度校准有机结合，MER-R1实现了二者优势的统一，突破了传统权衡困境，为推理驱动的智能系统提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: We find that explicit reasoning does not necessarily translate into better multimodal emotion recognition (MER) accuracy, even though it makes predictions more interpretable. Specifically, for reasoning-based MLLMs, fast thinking by triggering direct answers often outperforms slow thinking after deliberative reasoning. Our empirical analyses show that fast thinking improves recall with broader and more confident predictions, whereas slow thinking favors precision through conservative filtering of incorrect categories. Building on these insights, we propose MER-R1, a reinforcement learning framework that turns slow-fast complementarity into explicit optimization. Dual-objective disentanglement separates recall and precision into two optimization signals, allowing them to be jointly optimized rather than traded off against each other. Slow-fast confidence calibration further aligns the final slow-thinking answer with fast-thinking intuition, strengthening correct emotions while suppressing incorrect ones. In this way, MER-R1 unifies the recall-oriented intuition of fast thinking with the precision-oriented selectivity of slow thinking. We further provide theoretical justification for this synergy, showing that it mitigates variance-induced interference during optimization. Extensive experiments on MER-UniBench and MME-Emotion show that MER-R1 achieves state-of-the-art performance and makes reasoning genuinely benefit emotion recognition.

ToE integrates a reinforcement learning-driven multi-source retrieval agent, an evidence evaluation agent, and an argument tree aggregation algorithm to iteratively decompose, retrieve, and verify claims through an explainable evidence chain. We further provide a theoretical analysis of the retrieval process, deriving a formal error bound that guarantees the learned policy converges to a neighborhood of the information-theoretically optimal policy. Experiments across multiple datasets and backbone LLMs demonstrate that ToE achieves improvements ranging from 4 to 24 percentage points over competitive baselines, with particularly pronounced gains on adversarially poisoned inputs.

### [140] [Understanding Rollout Error in Graph World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27780)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究图世界模型（GWMs）在长时程滚动中的误差问题，提出统一的固定边与动态边框架，引入图值滚动边界和节点-边联合算子，并设计了误差感知的GWM方法，有效抑制长时程发散，适用于动态图滚动与代理规划任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统世界模型多用于向量或图像环境中的规划，但在由代理、工具、技能、路径和依赖关系构成的图结构环境中，局部预测误差可能局部停留或通过图传播，且当边为预测而非固定时，失败模式发生变化，因此需要针对图结构环境重新研究长时程滚动误差。

Method: 提出统一的固定边与动态边图世界模型框架，引入动作节点以支持节点、边和图级决策；建立图值滚动边界，分离拓扑引起的误差放大与模型引起的误差放大；设计节点-边联合算子用于动态边滚动；结合谱正则化、滚动一致性与关键节点加权，提出误差感知的GWM方法。

Result: 在合成拓扑和异构代理图测试平台中，滚动误差与规划遗憾随时间增长；当图结构演化时，动态边训练是必要的；误差感知GWM能有效防止长时程发散，同时保持预测精度；真实世界图基准测试表明，GWM最适合动态图滚动与代理规划，而专用图模型在静态或稀疏预测任务上仍具优势。

Abstract: World models are often used for planning by rolling learned dynamics forward. Many planning environments, however, are not vectors or images; they are graphs of agents, tools, skills, routes, and dependencies. In these settings, a local prediction error may stay local or spread through the graph, and the failure mode changes again when edges are predicted rather than fixed. This paper studies long-horizon rollout error in Graph World Models (GWMs). We formulate a unified fixed-edge and dynamic-edge GWM framework with action nodes for node-, edge-, and graph-level decisions. We develop graph-valued rollout bounds that separate topology-induced amplification from model-induced amplification, and we introduce a joint node-edge operator for dynamic-edge rollouts. Guided by the analysis, we propose Error-Aware GWM, which combines spectral regularization, rollout consistency, and critical-node weighting. Across synthetic topologies and heterogeneous agent-graph testbeds, rollout error and planning regret grow with horizon, dynamic-edge training is needed when structure evolves, and Error-Aware GWM prevents long-horizon divergence while preserving prediction accuracy. Real-world graph benchmarks clarify the scope of GWMs: they are most useful for dynamic graph rollout and agent planning, while specialized graph models remain strong on static or sparse prediction tasks.

### [141] [Grounded Iterative Language Planning: How Parameterized World Models Reduce Hallucination Propagation in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27806)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究比较了基于代理的语言智能体世界模型与参数化世界模型在图结构规划任务上的表现，提出了一种名为GILP的混合方法，结合了参数化模型的稳定性与LLM的灵活性。通过一致性门控机制，显著降低幻觉状态率（从0.176降至0.035），提升成功率（从0.668升至0.838），同时仅增加约22%的LLM调用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言智能体的世界模型存在幻觉问题，难以通过传统损失函数衡量错误；而参数化模型虽可量化误差但规划能力较弱。因此需要一种兼顾准确性和灵活性的方法。

Method: 提出Grounded Iterative Language Planning（GILP），利用小型参数化骨干网络提供有效动作、预测状态变化、风险和价值，结合LLM生成动作与想象的状态变化，并通过一致性门控判断是否需修正，实现两者的协同优化。

Result: 在真实GPT-4o-mini调用下，幻觉状态率由0.176降至0.035；在模拟器校准实验中，成功率从0.668提升至0.838，仅增加约22%的LLM调用开销。

Conclusion: GILP成功融合了参数化模型的稳健性与语言模型的灵活性，在保持高效的同时显著提升了规划可靠性与准确性，为复杂任务中的智能体设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: World models for language agents come in two useful forms. An agent-based world model calls an LLM API and reasons flexibly in language, but its errors appear as hallucinated state changes that are hard to score with ordinary regression losses. A parameterized world model is a trained transition predictor; its errors are easier to measure with quantities such as NodeMSE, delta accuracy, and validity accuracy, but it is usually weaker as a standalone planner. We compare these two families on four graph-structured planning benchmarks and introduce operational hallucination metrics for the agent-based case. The comparison motivates \textbf{Grounded Iterative Language Planning} (GILP), which trains only a small parameterized backbone and combines it with API-based agent reasoning. The backbone supplies valid actions, predicted state deltas, risk, and value; the LLM drafts an action and imagined delta; and a consistency gate asks for revision when the two disagree. On real GPT-4o-mini calls, GILP reduces hallucinated-state rate from 0.176 to 0.035. In calibrated simulator ablations, it raises success from 0.668 to 0.838 while adding only ~22% extra LLM calls.

### [142] [ATOD: Annealed Turn-aware On-policy Distillation for Multi-turn Autonomous Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27814)
*Qitai Tan,Zefang Zong,Yang Li,Peng Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATOD是一种混合在线蒸馏算法，结合了在策略蒸馏（OPD）和强化学习（RL）的优势，通过渐进式调度和转级不一致-不确定性重加权机制，在长时序交互任务中实现快速且持续的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，OPD虽能提供密集指导，但性能易饱和；而RL虽可探索更高奖励，但早期学习效率低。两者互补性未被充分利用，亟需一种融合二者优势的混合训练策略。

Method: 提出ATOD算法，采用渐进式OPD-RL调度：初期以OPD为主快速接近教师行为，随后逐步增强RL以驱动探索；引入Turn-level Disagreement-Uncertainty Reweighting（T-DUR），对高价值动作片段进行软增强，提升长轨迹中的监督质量。

Result: 在ALFWorld、WebShop和Search-QA三个基准上，ATOD在不同规模学生模型下均显著优于基线方法，平均成功率比OPD提升3.03点，比GRPO提升23.62点，并超越对应教师模型2.16点。

Conclusion: ATOD通过有效融合模仿学习与强化学习，实现了早期高效学习与后期持续优化的平衡，在长时序交互任务中展现出优越的性能与泛化能力。

Abstract: Training small language-model agents for long-horizon interactive tasks requires both fast imitation and reward-driven improvement. On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher guidance and typically improves rapidly in the early stage, but its gains saturate once the student approaches the teacher, limiting the final performance ceiling. Reinforcement learning (RL) directly optimizes environment rewards and encourages exploratory improvement toward a higher reward-defined ceiling, but sparse and delayed feedback makes early-stage learning much less efficient than OPD. In this paper, we propose ATOD (Annealed Turn-aware On-policy Distillation), a hybrid online distillation algorithm that explicitly exploits this complementarity. (1) ATOD uses an annealed OPD-RL schedule: OPD dominates early training to approach teacher-level behavior, while RL is gradually strengthened to drive reward-based exploration. (2) ATOD introduces Turn-level Disagreement-Uncertainty Reweighting (T-DUR), which softly amplifies high-utility turns and improves dense supervision in long trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-QA show that ATOD consistently outperforms competing post-training baselines: across the three student sizes, ATOD improves average success rate by 3.03 points over OPD and 23.62 points over GRPO, while surpassing the corresponding teacher models by 2.16 points.

</details>


### [143] [NormAct: A Benchmark for Hidden Social Norm Compliance in Embodied Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27826)
*Shiyun Zhao,Xinwei Song,Tianyu Guo,Xiaomeng Gao,Mingyuan Liu,Xu Han,Yuanyuan Zhang,Zhenliang Zhang,Xue Feng,Bo Dai*
